## Text Elements
Theres no H on the right side...
 ^S5V8m7hD

There are 2 separate instances of oxygen however this does not matter
as it is just telling us how the oxygen is bonded to the rest of them
SO IGNORE AND TREAT AS 1 ^2xYnih2X

The 2 comes from the subscript ^uAPkbIFs

The reduction half equation is ^aKdZzBkY

Find oxidation numbers (not charges) ^xpfYxPOo
